#include "program_base.hpp"

#include "hash.hpp"
#include "mmap/mmap.hpp"

#include "hpds/pstringops.hpp"
#define ELEM_SEPARATOR "\n\t\t\t"

namespace dbtoaster {
  
  /* Definitions of auxiliary maps for storing materialized views. */
  struct NATION_entry {
    long NATION_NATIONKEY; STRING_TYPE NATION_NAME; long NATION_REGIONKEY; STRING_TYPE NATION_COMMENT; long __av;  NATION_entry* nxt; NATION_entry* prv;
    explicit NATION_entry() : nxt(nullptr), prv(nullptr) { /*NATION_NATIONKEY = 0L; NATION_NAME = ""; NATION_REGIONKEY = 0L; NATION_COMMENT = ""; __av = 0L; */ }
    explicit NATION_entry(const long c0, const STRING_TYPE& c1, const long c2, const STRING_TYPE& c3, const long c4) { NATION_NATIONKEY = c0; NATION_NAME = c1; NATION_REGIONKEY = c2; NATION_COMMENT = c3; __av = c4; }
    NATION_entry(const NATION_entry& other) : NATION_NATIONKEY( other.NATION_NATIONKEY ), NATION_NAME( other.NATION_NAME ), NATION_REGIONKEY( other.NATION_REGIONKEY ), NATION_COMMENT( other.NATION_COMMENT ), __av( other.__av ), nxt( nullptr ), prv( nullptr ) {}
    FORCE_INLINE NATION_entry& modify(const long c0, const STRING_TYPE& c1, const long c2, const STRING_TYPE& c3) { NATION_NATIONKEY = c0; NATION_NAME = c1; NATION_REGIONKEY = c2; NATION_COMMENT = c3;  return *this; }
    template<class Archive>
    void serialize(Archive& ar, const unsigned int version) const 
    {
      ar << ELEM_SEPARATOR;
      DBT_SERIALIZATION_NVP(ar, NATION_NATIONKEY);
      ar << ELEM_SEPARATOR;
      DBT_SERIALIZATION_NVP(ar, NATION_NAME);
      ar << ELEM_SEPARATOR;
      DBT_SERIALIZATION_NVP(ar, NATION_REGIONKEY);
      ar << ELEM_SEPARATOR;
      DBT_SERIALIZATION_NVP(ar, NATION_COMMENT);
      ar << ELEM_SEPARATOR;
      DBT_SERIALIZATION_NVP(ar, __av);
    }
  };
  struct NATION_mapkey0123_idxfn {
    FORCE_INLINE static size_t hash(const NATION_entry& e) {
      size_t h = 0;
      hash_combine(h, e.NATION_NATIONKEY);
      hash_combine(h, e.NATION_NAME);
      hash_combine(h, e.NATION_REGIONKEY);
      hash_combine(h, e.NATION_COMMENT);
      return h;
    }
    FORCE_INLINE static bool equals(const NATION_entry& x, const NATION_entry& y) {
      return x.NATION_NATIONKEY == y.NATION_NATIONKEY && x.NATION_NAME == y.NATION_NAME && x.NATION_REGIONKEY == y.NATION_REGIONKEY && x.NATION_COMMENT == y.NATION_COMMENT;
    }
  };
  
  typedef MultiHashMap<NATION_entry,long,
    HashIndex<NATION_entry,long,NATION_mapkey0123_idxfn,true>
  > NATION_map;
  typedef HashIndex<NATION_entry,long,NATION_mapkey0123_idxfn,true> HashIndex_NATION_map_0123;
  
  struct SSB4_entry {
    long SN_REGIONKEY; long CN_REGIONKEY; STRING_TYPE PART_TYPE; DOUBLE_TYPE __av;  SSB4_entry* nxt; SSB4_entry* prv;
    explicit SSB4_entry() : nxt(nullptr), prv(nullptr) { /*SN_REGIONKEY = 0L; CN_REGIONKEY = 0L; PART_TYPE = ""; __av = 0.0; */ }
    explicit SSB4_entry(const long c0, const long c1, const STRING_TYPE& c2, const DOUBLE_TYPE c3) { SN_REGIONKEY = c0; CN_REGIONKEY = c1; PART_TYPE = c2; __av = c3; }
    SSB4_entry(const SSB4_entry& other) : SN_REGIONKEY( other.SN_REGIONKEY ), CN_REGIONKEY( other.CN_REGIONKEY ), PART_TYPE( other.PART_TYPE ), __av( other.__av ), nxt( nullptr ), prv( nullptr ) {}
    FORCE_INLINE SSB4_entry& modify(const long c0, const long c1, const STRING_TYPE& c2) { SN_REGIONKEY = c0; CN_REGIONKEY = c1; PART_TYPE = c2;  return *this; }
    template<class Archive>
    void serialize(Archive& ar, const unsigned int version) const 
    {
      ar << ELEM_SEPARATOR;
      DBT_SERIALIZATION_NVP(ar, SN_REGIONKEY);
      ar << ELEM_SEPARATOR;
      DBT_SERIALIZATION_NVP(ar, CN_REGIONKEY);
      ar << ELEM_SEPARATOR;
      DBT_SERIALIZATION_NVP(ar, PART_TYPE);
      ar << ELEM_SEPARATOR;
      DBT_SERIALIZATION_NVP(ar, __av);

  };
  struct SSB4_mapkey012_idxfn {
    FORCE_INLINE static size_t hash(const SSB4_entry& e) {
      size_t h = 0;
      hash_combine(h, e.SN_REGIONKEY);
      hash_combine(h, e.CN_REGIONKEY);
      hash_combine(h, e.PART_TYPE);

    FORCE_INLINE static bool equals(const SSB4_entry& x, const SSB4_entry& y) {
      return x.SN_REGIONKEY == y.SN_REGIONKEY && x.CN_REGIONKEY == y.CN_REGIONKEY && x.PART_TYPE == y.PART_TYPE;
    }
  };

      hash_combine(h, e.SN_REGIONKEY);
      return h;
    }
    FORCE_INLINE static bool equals(const SSB4_mORDERS4_entry& x, const SSB4_mORDERS4_entry& y) {
      return x.SSB4_mORDERSORDERS_ORDERKEY == y.SSB4_mORDERSORDERS_ORDERKEY && x.PART_TYPE == y.PART_TYPE && x.SN_REGIONKEY == y.SN_REGIONKEY;
    }
  };

    FORCE_INLINE SSB4_mCUSTOMER1_entry& modify0(const long c0) { SSB4_mCUSTOMERCUSTOMER_CUSTKEY = c0;  return *this; }

    {

      ar << ELEM_SEPARATOR;

    }

  /* Type definition providing a way to access the results of the sql program */
  struct tlq_t{
    struct timeval t0,t; long tT,tN,tS;
    tlq_t(): tN(0), tS(0) { gettimeofday(&t0,NULL); }
  
  /* Serialization Code */
    template<class Archive>
    void serialize(Archive& ar, const unsigned int version) const {
  
      ar << "\n";
      const SSB4_map& _SSB4 = get_SSB4();
      dbtoaster::serialize_nvp_tabbed(ar, STRING(SSB4), _SSB4, "\t");
  
    }
  
    /* Functions returning / computing the results of top level queries */
    const SSB4_map& get_SSB4() const {
      return SSB4;
    
    }
  
  protected:
  
    /* Data structures used for storing / computing top level queries */
    SSB4_map SSB4;
  
  };
  
  /* Type definition providing a way to incrementally maintain the results of the sql program */

    /* Trigger functions for table relations */
    void on_insert_NATION(const long nation_nationkey, const STRING_TYPE nation_name, const long nation_regionkey, const STRING_TYPE nation_comment) {
      NATION_entry e(nation_nationkey, nation_name, nation_regionkey, nation_comment, 1L);
      NATION.addOrDelOnZero(e,1L);
    }
    
    void unwrap_insert_NATION(const event_args_t& ea) {
      on_insert_NATION(*(reinterpret_cast<long*>(ea[0])), *(reinterpret_cast<STRING_TYPE*>(ea[1])), *(reinterpret_cast<long*>(ea[2])), *(reinterpret_cast<STRING_TYPE*>(ea[3])));
    }
    
    
    
    /* Trigger functions for stream relations */
    void on_insert_LINEITEM(const long lineitem_orderkey, const long lineitem_partkey, const long lineitem_suppkey, const long lineitem_linenumber, const DOUBLE_TYPE lineitem_quantity, const DOUBLE_TYPE lineitem_extendedprice, const DOUBLE_TYPE lineitem_discount, const DOUBLE_TYPE lineitem_tax, const STRING_TYPE& lineitem_returnflag, const STRING_TYPE& lineitem_linestatus, const date lineitem_shipdate, const date lineitem_commitdate, const date lineitem_receiptdate, const STRING_TYPE& lineitem_shipinstruct, const STRING_TYPE& lineitem_shipmode, const STRING_TYPE& lineitem_comment) {
      BEGIN_TRIGGER(exec_stats,"insert_LINEITEM")
      BEGIN_TRIGGER(ivc_stats,"insert_LINEITEM")
      {  ++tN;
        { //slice
          const HASH_RES_t h3 = SSB4_mLINEITEM1_mapkey0_idxfn::hash(se4.modify0(lineitem_orderkey));
          const HashIndex_SSB4_mLINEITEM1_map_0* i1 = static_cast<HashIndex_SSB4_mLINEITEM1_map_0*>(SSB4_mLINEITEM1.index[1]);
          HashIndex_SSB4_mLINEITEM1_map_0::IdxNode* n1 = &(i1->buckets_[h3 % i1->size_]);
          SSB4_mLINEITEM1_entry* e1;
          do if ((e1=n1->obj) && h3 == n1->hash && SSB4_mLINEITEM1_mapkey0_idxfn::equals(se4, *e1)) {
            long cn_regionkey = e1->CN_REGIONKEY;
            long v1 = e1->__av;
            { //slice
              const HASH_RES_t h2 = SSB4_mLINEITEM2_mapkey0_idxfn::hash(se3.modify0(lineitem_partkey));
              const HashIndex_SSB4_mLINEITEM2_map_0* i2 = static_cast<HashIndex_SSB4_mLINEITEM2_map_0*>(SSB4_mLINEITEM2.index[1]);
              HashIndex_SSB4_mLINEITEM2_map_0::IdxNode* n2 = &(i2->buckets_[h2 % i2->size_]);
              SSB4_mLINEITEM2_entry* e2;
              do if ((e2=n2->obj) && h2 == n2->hash && SSB4_mLINEITEM2_mapkey0_idxfn::equals(se3, *e2)) {
                STRING_TYPE part_type = e2->PART_TYPE;
                long v2 = e2->__av;

    void on_system_ready_event() {
      BEGIN_TRIGGER(exec_stats,"system_ready_event")
      BEGIN_TRIGGER(ivc_stats,"system_ready_event")
      {  
        SSB4_mCUSTOMER2.clear();
        { //foreach
          NATION_entry* e127 = NATION.head;
          while(e127){
            long ssb4_mcustomercustomer_nationkey = e127->NATION_NATIONKEY;
            STRING_TYPE cn_name = e127->NATION_NAME;
            long cn_regionkey = e127->NATION_REGIONKEY;
            STRING_TYPE cn_comment = e127->NATION_COMMENT;
            long v127 = e127->__av;
            SSB4_mCUSTOMER2.addOrDelOnZero(se211.modify(ssb4_mcustomercustomer_nationkey,cn_regionkey),v127);
            e127 = e127->nxt;
          }
        }
      }
      END_TRIGGER(exec_stats,"system_ready_event")
      END_TRIGGER(ivc_stats,"system_ready_event")
    }

  /* Type definition providing a way to execute the sql program */
  class Program : public ProgramBase
  {
    public:
      Program(int argc = 0, char* argv[] = 0) : ProgramBase(argc,argv) {
        data.register_data(*this);
        
        /* Specifying data sources */
        
        pair<string,string> source1_adaptor_params[] = { make_pair("delimiter","|"), make_pair("schema","long,string,long,string") };
        std::shared_ptr<csv_adaptor> source1_adaptor(new csv_adaptor(get_relation_id("NATION"),2,source1_adaptor_params));
        frame_descriptor source1_fd("\n");
        std::shared_ptr<dbt_file_source> source1_file(new dbt_file_source("/Users/dashti/Documents/MyWorkspaces/DATASRC/dbtoaster/experiments/data/tpch/standard/nation.csv",source1_fd,source1_adaptor));
        add_source(source1_file, true);
        
        pair<string,string> source2_adaptor_params[] = { make_pair("delimiter","|"), make_pair("schema","long,long,long,long,double,double,double,double,string,string,date,date,date,string,string,string") };
        std::shared_ptr<csv_adaptor> source2_adaptor(new csv_adaptor(get_relation_id("LINEITEM"),2,source2_adaptor_params));
        frame_descriptor source2_fd("\n");
        std::shared_ptr<dbt_file_source> source2_file(new dbt_file_source("/Users/dashti/Documents/MyWorkspaces/DATASRC/dbtoaster/experiments/data/tpch/standard/lineitem.csv",source2_fd,source2_adaptor));
        add_source(source2_file);
        
        pair<string,string> source3_adaptor_params[] = { make_pair("delimiter","|"), make_pair("schema","long,long,string,double,date,string,string,long,string") };
        std::shared_ptr<csv_adaptor> source3_adaptor(new csv_adaptor(get_relation_id("ORDERS"),2,source3_adaptor_params));
        frame_descriptor source3_fd("\n");
        std::shared_ptr<dbt_file_source> source3_file(new dbt_file_source("/Users/dashti/Documents/MyWorkspaces/DATASRC/dbtoaster/experiments/data/tpch/standard/orders.csv",source3_fd,source3_adaptor));
        add_source(source3_file);
        
        pair<string,string> source4_adaptor_params[] = { make_pair("delimiter","|"), make_pair("schema","long,string,string,string,string,long,string,double,string") };
        std::shared_ptr<csv_adaptor> source4_adaptor(new csv_adaptor(get_relation_id("PART"),2,source4_adaptor_params));
        frame_descriptor source4_fd("\n");
        std::shared_ptr<dbt_file_source> source4_file(new dbt_file_source("/Users/dashti/Documents/MyWorkspaces/DATASRC/dbtoaster/experiments/data/tpch/standard/part.csv",source4_fd,source4_adaptor));
        add_source(source4_file);
        
        pair<string,string> source5_adaptor_params[] = { make_pair("delimiter","|"), make_pair("schema","long,string,string,long,string,double,string,string") };
        std::shared_ptr<csv_adaptor> source5_adaptor(new csv_adaptor(get_relation_id("CUSTOMER"),2,source5_adaptor_params));
        frame_descriptor source5_fd("\n");
        std::shared_ptr<dbt_file_source> source5_file(new dbt_file_source("/Users/dashti/Documents/MyWorkspaces/DATASRC/dbtoaster/experiments/data/tpch/standard/customer.csv",source5_fd,source5_adaptor));
        add_source(source5_file);
        
        pair<string,string> source6_adaptor_params[] = { make_pair("delimiter","|"), make_pair("schema","long,string,string,long,string,double,string") };
        std::shared_ptr<csv_adaptor> source6_adaptor(new csv_adaptor(get_relation_id("SUPPLIER"),2,source6_adaptor_params));
        frame_descriptor source6_fd("\n");
        std::shared_ptr<dbt_file_source> source6_file(new dbt_file_source("/Users/dashti/Documents/MyWorkspaces/DATASRC/dbtoaster/experiments/data/tpch/standard/supplier.csv",source6_fd,source6_adaptor));
        add_source(source6_file);
  
      }
  
      /* Imports data for static tables and performs view initialization based on it. */
      void init() {
          //P0_PLACE_HOLDER
          table_multiplexer.init_source(run_opts->batch_size, run_opts->parallel, true);
          stream_multiplexer.init_source(run_opts->batch_size, run_opts->parallel, false);
          process_tables();
          data.on_system_ready_event();
          //P2_PLACE_HOLDER
      }
  
      /* Saves a snapshot of the data required to obtain the results of top level queries. */
      snapshot_t take_snapshot(){
          tlq_t* d = new tlq_t((tlq_t&)data);
          if (d->tS==0) { gettimeofday(&(d->t),NULL); d->tT=((d->t).tv_sec-(d->t0).tv_sec)*1000000L+((d->t).tv_usec-(d->t0).tv_usec); } printf("SAMPLE=standard,%ld,%ld,%ld\n",d->tT,d->tN,d->tS);
          return snapshot_t( d );
      }
  
    protected:
      data_t data;
  };
  class Tpchssb4 : public Program
  {
    public:
      Tpchssb4(int argc = 0, char* argv[] = 0) : Program(argc,argv) {
      }
  };

}
